# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

I've successfully completed the comprehensive search for the Grafana query result cache architecture and created the answer file. Here's what I found:

## Summary of Findings

I've identified **24 Go source files** implementing the query caching layer in grafana/grafana across these key areas:

### 1. **Cache Service Interface** (pkg/services/caching/)
- `CachingService` interface defining the caching contract
- `OSSCachingService` (no-op implementation)
- `CachingServiceClient` wrapper with `WithQueryDataCaching()` method
- Cache key generation via `GetKey()` using SHA256 hash of JSON-serialized queries

### 2. **Cache Storage Backends** (pkg/infra/remotecache/)
- **Redis**: Full Redis support with TLS, authentication, connection pooling
- **Memcached**: Memcached storage implementation
- **Database**: Cache stored in `cache_data` table with automatic garbage collection (10-minute cleanup job)
- **Encryption & Prefix** wrappers for composable cache behavior

### 3. **Cache TTL Policy** (Dashboard Panels)
- `QueryCachingTTL` field in panel specifications across v2alpha1, v2beta1 schema versions
- Configuration propagated through dashboard migration converters

### 4. **Cache Invalidation** (Dashboard Save Events)
- `DashboardActivityChannel` interface for dashboard save/delete events
- `DashboardHandler.DashboardSaved()` broadcasts events when dashboards are saved
- Events can trigger cache invalidation for panel queries

### 5. **Cache Middleware**
- `CachingMiddleware` integrates caching into plugin handler chain
- Intercepts QueryData requests to check/update cache

### 6. **Metrics & Configuration**
- Prometheus histograms for cache hit/miss/error tracking
- Remote cache configuration via settings file

Uses UPSERT pattern (INSERT with UPDATE fallback) to handle concurrent updates.\\n\\nThe RemoteCache class (pkg/infra/remotecache/remotecache.go) abstracts these backends and provides optional encryption wrapper (encryptedCacheStorage) and key prefix wrapper (prefixCacheStorage) for composable cache behavior.\\n\\n## Cache TTL Policy (Dashboard Panels)\\n\\nQuery caching TTL is configured at the panel level through the QueryCachingTTL field defined in:\\n- pkg/kinds/dashboard/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n- apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v2beta1/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n- apps/dashboard/pkg/apis/dashboard/v2alpha1/dashboard_spec_gen.go\\n\\nThe migration conversion files (apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/conversion/) handle backward compatibility when converting between dashboard schema versions (v1beta1, v2alpha1, v2beta1).\\n\\n## Cache Invalidation on Dashboard Save\\n\\nDashboard save events trigger cache invalidation through the DashboardActivityChannel interface.
